				<h2 class='wrapper essays-heading pt-10 pb-10 text-left'>
				Get Groceries Delivered at your Doorstep! Contact the Nearest Grocery Stores in Selaiyur, Chennai!
				</h2>
				<div class='wrapper essays-content '><p>There are times when getting out of the house or the busy routine to buy grocery seems next to impossible. At such times, getting grocery delivered at your doorstep sounds like a perfect hassle-free solution and time-saver. Grocery stores in Selaiyur, Chennai these days offer a wide range of basic home utility products like food, kitchenware, toiletries as well as personal beauty products all under one roof. Hence buying grocery becomes convenient. Let us have a look at the different products offered by grocery stores in Selaiyur Chennai.</p>
<p>You will find a wide range of products in different grocery stores</p>
<p><strong>Grocery and Other Staples</strong> like dals and pulses, rice and rice products, flour, grains, sugar, salt, oil, ghee, etc.<p>
<p><strong>Dairy and Beverages</strong> including cheese and butter</p>
<p><strong>Frozen Food Products </strong> like peas, paneer, corn, etc.</p>
<p><strong>Packaged Food Products </strong> like biscuits, snacks, ketchup, pasta, ready to cook, sweets, pickle, etc.</p>
<p><strong>Home and Kitchen Products </strong>like detergents, fabric cleaners, utensil cleaners, napkins, kitchen tools, home utility, etc.</p>
<p><h3>Delivery Services</h3></p>
<p>Grocery shops Selaiyur, Chennai has, are offering delivery services amidst the coronavirus lockdown. These services are offered during a specific time slot every day. Keeping safety and hygiene at priority all the grocery shops are taking all the necessary measures mentioned in the guidelines by the government as well as WHO to ensure safe grocery home delivery services. Moreover, as a safety measure, many stores are accepting only online payments for home delivery services. Also, note that since the situation is getting critical day by day most grocery shops can deliver only essential food products.</p>
<p><h3>Delivery Charges</h3></p>
<p>The delivery charges vary from one grocery store to the other while a majority don’t charge additional delivery charges. It is always best to inquire about the same with the respective Selaiyur, Chennai grocery store.</p>
<p><h3>Things to Keep in Mind Before Buying Grocery</h3></p>
<p>While choosing a grocery store nearby following key pointers must be considered:</p>
<p>The type, brands, and quality of grocery products offered.</p>
<p>The popularity of the grocery store in Selaiyur Chennai.</p>
<p>The reviews and ratings from the previous customers with regard to the quality and service provided.</p>
<p>The different types of after-sales services offered.</p>
<p>The discounts offered by the respective grocery shop</p>
